Their are four types of people accepted into the spartan 4 program each with their own distinct traits and personalities - Personalities similar to our own. 1. The prodigy: These are individuals who are naturally gifted in a certain field that enables them to advance faster than most before becoming spartans - Think Olympia Vale. 2. The leader: These individuals are gifted in the art of combat tactics and situational analysis, they can easily adapt to any given situation, enabling them to lead their allies to victory- Think Edward Buck, Gabriel Thorn, and Jameson Lock. 3. The Specialist: These are individuals who possess an exceptional level of skill  in their respective fields - Think Naya Rey (Signal intelligence) and Holly Tenaka (Engineering). 4. The battle harden warrior: These are individuals who have proven themselves capable of going toe to toe with foes more powerful than themselves single handedly- Think Sarah Palmer (who killed a brute chieftain by herself) or Frank Kodiak (Who killed a sword wielding elite during the covenant war)

This is a beautiful trailer on many levels:  - The drill sergeant becomes relatable, and is a great conduit for the viewer, experienced Halo veterans and green rookies anew, showing how personal her respect and love for the SPARTANs are.  - The SPARTANs themselves are tough, but not invincible, mythical and yet human, warriors yet humble - they can get hurt, but the focus is to work as a team, to deliver hope.  - The music, pacing, atmosphere, worldbuilding is simple, without unneeded exposition, and shows without telling in a good way.   - This is how you show Halo for the younger, new generation, while at the same time respecting the older community.
